\meaning{\arthanonum{parxtiyoMdu sathxladalilxyU uLida aidu sathxlagaLive. udAharaNege Bakatxnalilx maheVsha, Bakatxnalilx parxsAdi, Bakatxnalilx pArxNaliMgi, Bakatxnalilx sharaNa, Bakatxnalilx aikayx, hAgeyeV maheVshanalilx Bakatx, maheVshanalilx parxsAdi, itAyxdi. alalxde, parxtiyoMdu sathxladalilxyU tananx sathxlada liMgavananxlalxde, A liMgadalilxruva uLida aidu liMgagaLanUnx sAdhakanu apiRsa\-beVku. udAharaNege, Bakatxnu AcAraliMgavanUnx, Bakatxnalilxruva maheVshanu AcAra\-liMgadalilxruva guruliMgavanUnx, Bakatxnalilxruva parxsAdiyu AcAraliMgadalilxruva shivaliMgavanUnx, Bakatxnalilxruva pArxNaliMgiyu AcAraliMgadalilxruva jaMgamaliMgavanUnx, Bakatxnalilxruva sharaNanu AcAraliMgadalilxruva parxsAdaliMgavanUnx, Bakatxnalilxruva aikayxnu AcAraliMgadalilxruva mahAliMgavanUnx aciRsabeVku. Bakatxnige paqthivxyeV aMga, A aMgakekx sucitatxveMba sUkaSxmX hasatx. Bakatxnalilx maheVsha, parxsAdi, itAyxdi iruvaMte, avana aMgavAda paqthivxyalilx maheVshana aMgavAda apupx, parxsAdiya aMgavAda aginx, itAyxdi aMgagaLU, sucitatxveMba hasatxdalilx nirahaMkAra sumana, muMtAda hasatxgaLU ive. hiVge vAsatxvavAgi liMgagaLu AralalxveMdU, sathxlagaLu AralalxveMdU, deVhagaLu Aralalx\-veMdU, oMdeV liMga, oMdeV sathxla, oMdeV deVha eMdU tiLidu adanunx oDagUDidavaneV SaTfsathxlabarxhimx athavA barxhamxyoVgi.}
\ullekha{basaveVshavxradeVvaru taqNapuruSana... iMtapapx SaTfsathxlabarxhimxge namoV namoV eMbe... (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 1386-493); AkAravadu iSaTxliMga... (savasaM. 5; akakxma. 209-61); guruliMgajaMgamavanu BinanxviTaTxridare... iMtu aSATxvaraNa BinanxviTuTx SaTfsathxlabarxhimxyAdeneMdare... (savasaM. 12; deVshikeVM. 167-50).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}

\meaning{\arthanonum{SaDaBxvavikAragaLU saha AdhAyxtimxka jiVvanada veYrigaLeV. avugaLu nashisada horatu mukitx sAdhayxvilalx. vacanakAraru avugaLanunx keDisuva upAyavanunx hiVge tiLisidAdxre: nAnu savxtaMtarx asitxtavxvanunx paDedidedxVne eMdu tiLiyade nAnu guruvina kaqpAgaBaRdalilxdedxVneMdu tiLidare, asitx eMba vikAra keDutatxde. nAnu mAyeya pariNAmadiMda huTiTx\-dedxVne eMdu BAvisade, nAnu gurukarasaMjAta eMdu BAvisidare, \hbox{jAyate} eMba vikAra keDutatxde. guruvu anugarxhisida sadABxvajAta liMgavanunx aMgadalilx dharisuva mUlaka taqpitxyanunx saMpAdisi, adariMda vipariNamateV eMba vikAravanunx keDisabahudu. guruvu toVrisikoTaTx AcAra matutx jAcnxnamAgaRdalilx naDedu AdhAyxtamxdalilx beLeyuva mUlaka vivadhaRte eMba vikAravanunx suDabahudu. deVheVMdirxyAdigaLelalx nananxvalalx, parashiva\-navu eMdu elalxvanUnx parashivanige apiRsuva mUlaka apakiSxVyate eMba vikAravanunx keDisabahudu. maNiNxnalilx liVyavAguva badalu liMgAMga aikayxda mUlaka liMgadalilx liVyavAdare, vinashayxti eMba vikAravanunx keDisabahudu. (noVDi. SaDABxva vikAra)}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{SaDivxdha}
\medskip

\begin{shl}
sharaNa tananx pArxrabadhxkamaR tiVrida visAtxravanariya,\\
parxkAshisutitxdadx kAraNa,\\
shAvxna jaMgamarUpenabeVkAyitutx,\\
gaja matiyiMda puradalilxge baMdu, A puradalilx eSuTx\\
suKavAgidadxrU miVgemige tananx matiyane nenevutipupxdu,\\
A jaMgama modalu parabarxhamxdiMda deVhaviDidanAgi,\\
A deVhadalilx eSuTx suKavAgidadxreyU\\
migemige A parabarxhamxne nenevutihanu,\\
idu kAraNa, shAvxna gaja iveraDU sharaMge,\\
jaMgamasavxrUpenabeVkAyitutx,\\
manave makaRTa, arive pi[piV]lika,\\
mahAjAcnxnave vihaMga, nitayx ecacxrava kukukxTa,\\
tananx tAnarivude shAvxna, tananx budidhxye gava,\\
iMtiV SaDivxdhava balAlxtane barxhamxjAcnxni\\
nimAmxNe, nimamx parxmatharANi,\\
gUheVshavxrapirxya baMkaNaNxniTaTx muMDigeyanetutxvarilalx,\\
basavapirxya mahAparxBuve.
\end{shl}
\smallskip
\newmeaning{\artha{rUpa, darxvayx, padAthaR, sAnxna, maMtarx, taqpitx.}}
\newmeaning{\artha{AcAra, guru, liMga, jaMgama, pAdoVdaka, parxsAda.}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
\word{SaDivxdha AcAraliMga}
\meaning{\arthanonum{misharxSaDusathxla sidAdhxMtada parxkAra, parxtiyoMdu aMgasathxladalilxyU uLida aMgasathxlagaLu aDakavAgive. udAharaNege: Bakatxna Bakatx, Bakatxna maheVsha, Bakatxna parxsAdi, Bakatxna pArxNaliMgi, Bakatxna sharaNa matutx Bakatxna aikayx. hAgeyeV parxtiyoMdu aMgasathxladalilxyU uLida aMgasathxlagaLu aDakavAgive. AcAradalilx AcAraliMga, AcAradalilx guruliMga, AcAradalilx shivaliMga, AcAradalilx jaMgamaliMga, AcAradalilx parxsAdaliMga, AcAradalilx mahAliMga. hiVgAdare Bakatxnu AcAraliMgavanunx sAkASxtakxrisikoLuLxvudeMdare, Aru liMgagaLanUnx sAkASxtakxrisikoLuLxvudeMdathaR. hAge sAkASxtakxrisikoLaLxlu avanu Bakatxsathxladalilx naDedukoMDaMte naDedukoMDare sAladu, adara jotege uLida aidU sathxlagaLa sAdhakanaMte AcarisabeVkAgutatxde. adu heVgeMbudanunx SaDivxdha AcAraliMga parikalapxneyu tiLisutatxde. AcAraliMgada AcAra\-liMgavanunx taqpitxpaDisalu avanu paMcAcAra niratanAgabeVku. (noVDi. paMcAcAra), AcAraliMgadalilxna guruliMgavanunx olisikoLaLxlu sadA paMcAkaSxri maMtarxvanunx ucacxrisutitxrabeVku, AcAraliMgadalilxruva shivaliMgavanunx olisikoLaLxlu, pUjA samayadalilx tadeVka daqSiTxyiMda iSaTxliMgavanunx niriVkiSxsabeVku. AcAradalilxruva jaMgamaliMgavanunx sAkASxtakxrisikoLaLxlu, avanu yajacnx (dAsoVha) mADabeVku. aSaTxvidhAcaRne matutx SoVDashoVpacAragaLanUnx mADabeVku. (noVDi. dAdoVha, aSaTxvidhAcaRne, SoVDa\-shoVpacAra), AcAraliMgadalilxna parxsAdaliMgavanunx taqpitxpaDisalu para\-shiva\-nanunx kuritu yAvAgalU sotxVtarx mADabeVku; AcAraliMgadoLagina mahAliMgavanunx sAkASxtakxrisikoLaLxlu, mahAliMgavanunx veVdhisi, tAnu adaralilx aikayxvAgabeVku. hiVge SaDivxdha AcAraliMgavu kirxye, maMtarx, niriVkaSxNe, yajana, Ishana, (sotxVtarx) matutx veVdhA eMba Aru kirxyegaLanunx oLagoMDide.}
\ullekha{SaDivxdha AcAraliMga -ivu kirxye, maMtarx, niriVkaSxNa, yajana, ILana, veVdhA eMdirutatxve. AcAraliMgada Aru vidhada parxgatigaLu ililx heVLalapxTiTxve (shivAkoV. 61-70).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}

\meaning{\arthanonum{guNavuLaLx parashiva. parashivanige aneVka guNagaLive. parxpaMcavanunx saqSiTxsuva, rakiSxsuva matutx saMharisuva shakitxyide, janaranunx avaravara kamaRgaLige takakxMte shikiSxsuva athavA anugarxhisuva shakitx ide. hiVge shakitx eMba guNa avanigide. alalxde, avanu satf, citf, AnaMda, nitayx matutx paripUNaR. shaMkarAcAyaRra parabarxhamxnU satf, citf, AnaMda, nitayx matutx anaMtaneV AdarU, avanige yAva riVtiya shakitxyU ilalxvAdudariMda avanu niguRNa.}}

\begin{entry}
\word{saguNa niguRNa}
\meaning{\arthanonum{shaMkarAcAyaRra cidadevxYtada parxkAra satf, citf, AnaMdaneV parama satayx athavA parabarxhamx. iMtha parabarxhamxnige yAvudeV riVtiya AkAra (doDaDxdu, saNaNxdu) yAvudeV riVtiya guNagaLAgali (keMpu, kapupx itAyxdi) ilalx. I kAraNadiMda avananunx niguRNa, nirAkAra barxhamxneMdu kareyutAtxre. shaMkarAcAyaRra parxkAra I riVtiya citfsavxrUpanAda \hbox{niguRNa} barxhamx mAtarx satayx, jagatUtx, jagatatxnunx saqSiTxsida IshavxranU, jiVvagaLU asatayx. avideyxya deseyiMdAgi nAvu Ishavxranu (saguNa barxhamxnu) jagatatxnunx saqSiTxsutAtxneMdu BarxmisutetxVve. vAsatxvavAgi jagatUtx ilalx, jagatatxnunx saqSiTxsa\-beVkAda IshavxranU ilalx. katatxlalilx hagagxvu hAvinaMte heVge kANutatxdeyoV hAgeyeV ajAcnxnigaLige niguRNa barxhamxneV jagatAtxgi kANutatxde. Adare vacanakArara parxkAra, parashivanu modalu aMdare shUnayxsithxtiyalilxruvAga, niguRNa\-nAgirutAtxne hAgU avaneV saqSiTx mADidAga saguNanAgutAtxne. shaMkarAcAyaRra parxkAra parabarxhamxnanunx noVDidavarige jagatutx kANuvudilalx. avarige kANuvudelalx niguRNa barxhamxneV, adeV riVti jagatatxnunx kANuvavarige niguRNa barxhamx kANuvudilalx. hiVge oMdeV vasutxvanunx eraDu koVnagaLiMda-avideyx\-yiMdAgi vAyxvahArika koVnadiMda matutx jAcnxna pArxpitxyiMdAgi pAramAthiRka daqSiTxyiMda noVDalu sAdhayxvideyeV horatu, vAsatxvikavAgi EkakAladalilx eraDu satayxgaLilalx. Adare vacanakArara parxkAra, obabxneV parashivanu vAsatxvika\-vAgi oMdu kAladalilx shUnayxdaMte, matotxMdu kAladalilx saguNabarxhamxnaMte, hAgU kelavu veVLe jagatitxnaMte kANutAtxne. shiva jagavAgalU balalx, jagavAgadiralU balalx. Adare ivelalx avana vividha avasethxgaLeV vinA, namamx vayxkitxniSaThx BarxmegaLalalx. (11:23)}
\ullekha{ayAyx, samasatx mAyAbaleyalilx, janamxjanAmxMtaravetatxtoLali baLali... SoVDashavaNaR, dAvxdashAcAra, saguNaniguRNaliVleya karuNisi... (savasaM. 3; cenanxba. 935-298); nitAyxnaMdasaMvitapxrXBAmUtiRyAda... saguNaniguRNasaninxhita sadamalAnaMda... (savaaM. 12; deVshikeVM. 342-1105).}}

\newmeaning{\arthanonum{Adare, vacanakArara parxkAra, parxpaMcadalilxruva elalx vasutxgaLU shakitx\-yiMda mADalapxTiTxve. \newmeaning{\artha{mUraneya athaRdalilx sathxlavu sAdhakana AdhAyxtimxka haMtakekx anavxyisutatxde. \ullekha{sahajadiMda nirAlaMbavAyitutx... ivarelalx namamx guheVshavxrana karasathxlada haMginalilx huTiTx beLedaru... \begin{entry}

\begin{entry}

\meaning{\arthanonum{nUroMdu sathxlagaLalilx oMdu; liMgavu aikayxnalilx aikayxnu liMgadalilx Binanx BAvavilalxde paramAnaMda pArxpitxyanunx hoMduva sathxla; koMDudu parxsAdisathxla.}
\ullekha{iMtu parxkAshaliMga tirxvidhaveVkavAda liMgameYkayxnalilx pariNAmaparigArxhamaM paDedumAtanumA liMgadalilx pariNAma gArxhakatavxmaM paDedu BinanxBAvaparitAyxgadiMde paramAnaMda pariNAmatavxmaM pArxpatxBeVdaveMtidiRtetxMdoDe muMde sivxVkaqtaparxsAdasathxlavAdudu (keYvasha. 157-1 sUtarxM).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}

\meaning{\arthanonum{liMgaSaTAkxMtagaRta aikayxsathxlada oMbatutx vidha avAMtara sathxlagaLalilx oMdu. jAcnxnaparxkAshasaMpananxnAda shivayoVgiya sathxla. jAcnxnaparxkAsha saMpananxnAda shivayoVgiyalilx jiVvAtamx-paramAtamx rUpavAda muKAyxthaRviruvudilalx (aMga-liMgagaLalilx aupAdhikaBeVdavanunx heVLuvudu muKAyxthaR). I BeVdavanunx aLidu nirupAdhigaLAda aMga-liMgagaLalilxna ceYtanayxgaLa sAmarasayxvanunx boVdhisuvudeV lakaSxNAthaR. (nirupAdhigaLAda aMga-liMgagaLa nitayx aikayxrUpavAda lakaSxNAthaRvU iruvudilalx). I vAcAyxthaR-lakaSxNAthaRgaLa vicAragaLanunx aritu lakaSxyXvanunx pArxpitxmADikoMDa naMtara liMgAMga sAmarasayxda anuBUta rUpavAda parxsAdavanunx sivxVkarisuvudeV sivxVkaqtaparxsAdisathxla.}}

\meaning{\arthanonum{manuSayxnu ajAcnxnadiMdAgi, tananx nijavAda guriyeVneMbudanunx maretu, deVha matutx iMdirxyagaLa saluvAgi aneVka riVtiya kamaRgaLanunx mADi badadhxkanAgidAdxne. I sithxtiyalilx kamiR matutx saMsAragaLa naDuve baMdhavide. Adare tAnAreMbudanunx tiLidu, tananx matutx parashivana naDuve saMbaMdhavanenxVpaRDisikoMDare, Aga A saMbaMdha subadadhx (oLeLxya saMbaMdha)venisikoLuLxtatxde.}
\ullekha{pUvaRkekx tALAgi utatxrakekx talahA... nibadidhxya kArukana keYyalilx subadidhxsi, shudedhxYsi... (savasaM. 6; okakxli. 1739-659); lakaSxda meVle toMbatAtxrusAvira... badadhxkatanavanu subadadhxva mADade... (savasaM. 8; moVLimA. 2096-675).}}
\end{entry}

\begin{entry}
